三棱草	sān léng cǎo； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">پىيىزەك</p>\n\n
三棱草香附子	三棱草／香附子（沙草科）； sān léng cǎo xiāng fù zǐ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سۇ ھىدى، ھىندى، توڭقۇز تېرىقى؛ مىسىل، سۇ ھىدى ھىندى</p>\n\n
三棱针	sān léng zhēn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قىرلىق قان ئېلىش يىڭنىسى، ئۈچ قىرلىق نەشتەر</p>\n\n
三棱镜	sān léng jìng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">پرىزما، ئۈچ قىرلىق ئەينەك؛ ئۈچ قىرلىق پرىزما</p>\n\n
三棱鸢尾	sān léng yuān wěi； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئىرىس پرىزماتىكا قۇشى</p>\n\n
三槽板	sān cáo bǎn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئېرىقچىلىق تاختا</p>\n\n
三槽苘麻	sān cáo  má； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئېرىقچىلىق كېۋەز ئانىسى</p>\n\n
三模冗余	sān mó rǒng yú； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ مودۇل قالدۇقى</p>\n\n
三次产业	sān cì chǎn yè； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">3 كەسىپ</p>\n\n
三次多项式	sān cì duō xiàng shì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ دەرىجىلىك كۆپ ئەزالىق</p>\n\n
三次幂	sān cì mì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچىنچى دەرىجە؛ كۇب، ئۈچىنچى دەرىجىلىك</p>\n\n
三次挠线	sān cì náo xiàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچىنچى تەرتىپلىك ئەگرى سىزىق</p>\n\n
三次方程	sān cì fāng chéng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچىنچى دەرىجىلىك تەڭلىمە، كۇب دەرىجىلىك تەڭلىمە</p>\n\n
三次曲线	sān cì qǔ xiàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچىنچى تەرتىپلىك ئەگرى سىزىق</p>\n\n
三次曲面	sān cì qǔ miàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچىنچى تەرتىپلىك سىرت</p>\n\n
三次样条函数	sān cì yàng tiáo hán shù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچىنچى تەرتىپلىك سپلايىن فۇنكسىيە</p>\n\n
三次根	sān cì gēn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچىنچى دەرىجىلىك يىلتىز</p>\n\n
三次结婚	sān cì jié hūn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ نىكاھلىق بولۇش</p>\n\n
三次绕组	sān cì rào zǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلەمچى ئورام گۇرۇپپىسى</p>\n\n
三次谐波	sān cì xié bō； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلەمچى گارمونىك دولقۇن</p>\n\n
三次谐波电动势	sān cì xié bō diàn dòng shì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلەمچى گارمونىك دولقۇنلۇق ئېلېكتر يۈرگۈزگۈچى كۈچ</p>\n\n
三次谐波电流	sān cì xié bō diàn liú； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلەمچى گارمونىك دولقۇنلۇق توك</p>\n\n
三次谐波绕组	sān cì xié bō rào zǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلەمچى گارمونىك دولقۇنلۇق ئورام گۇرۇپپىسى</p>\n\n
三步态的	sān bù tai de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ خىل يۈرۈش</p>\n\n
三步舞	sān bù wǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قەدەملىك تانسا</p>\n\n
三歧纳塞拉草	sān qí nà sāi lā cǎo； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئاچا ناسسېللا ئوتى</p>\n\n
三歧肠类	sān qí cháng lèi； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئاچا ئۈچەيلىكلەر</p>\n\n
三段学说	sān duàn xué shuō； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ باسقۇچ فورمۇلىسى تەلىماتى</p>\n\n
三段式	sān duàn shì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">3 باسقۇچ فورمۇلىسى؛ ئۈچ باسقۇچ فورمۇلىسى</p>\n\n
三段式咏叹调	sān duàn shì yǒng tàn diào； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ باسقۇچلۇق ئارىيە</p>\n\n
三段式学说	sān duàn shì xué shuō； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">3 باسقۇچ فورمۇلىسى تەلىماتى</p>\n\n
三段律	sān duàn lǜ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">3 باسقۇچ قانۇنىيىتى؛ ئۈچ باسقۇچ قانۇنىيىتى</p>\n\n
三段论	sān duàn lùn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سىللوگىزم؛ ئۈچ باسقۇچلۇق يەكۈن نەزەرىيىسى؛ 3 باسقۇچلۇق يەكۈن نەزەرىيىسى؛ ئۈچ ھۆكۈملۈك</p>\n\n
三段论专家	sān duàn lùn zhuān jiā； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سىللوگىست</p>\n\n
三段论体系	sān duàn lùn tǐ xì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سىللوگىستىكا؛ ئۈچ ھۆكۈملۈك سىستېمىسى</p>\n\n
三段论推理	sān duàn lùn tuī lǐ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سىللوگىستىك ئەقلىي خۇلاسە؛ ئۈچ ھۆكۈملۈك ئەقلىي خۇلاسە</p>\n\n
三段论法	sān duàn lùn fǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سىللوگىزم؛ ئۈچ ھۆكۈملۈك ئۇسۇلى</p>\n\n
三段论的素材	sān duàn lùn de sù cái； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ھۆكۈملۈكنىڭ خام ماتېرىيالى</p>\n\n
三毛滴虫属	sān máo dī chóng shǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىخوموناس تامچە قۇرتى ئۇرۇقدىشى</p>\n\n
三毛草	三毛草（禾本科）； sān máo cǎo； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">بېتىگە</p>\n\n
三毛草属	sān máo cǎo shǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">بېتىگە ئۇرۇقدىشى</p>\n\n
三民主义	sān mín zhǔ yì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ مەسلەك</p>\n\n
三氟三氯乙烷	sān fú sān lǜ yǐ wán； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىفتوروترىخلوروئېتان</p>\n\n

三氟氯乙烯树脂	sān fú lǜ yǐ xī shù zhī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىفتوروخلورېتىلېن سمولىسى</p>\n\n

三氯乙酸	sān lǜ yǐ suān； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىخلوروئاتسېتىك كىسلاتا</p>\n\n
三氯化氮	sān lǜ huà dàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئازوت ترىخلورىد</p>\n\n
三氯化氮处理	sān lǜ huà dàn chǔ lǐ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئازوت ترىخلورىد ئارقىلىق بىر تەرەپ قىلىش</p>\n\n
三氯化物	sān lǜ huà wù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىخلورىد</p>\n\n

三氯苯	sān lǜ běn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىخلوروبېنزېن</p>\n\n
三氯苯氧基醋酸，三氯苯氧基乙酸	sān lǜ běn yǎng jī cù suān , sān lǜ běn yǎng jī yǐsuān； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىخلوروفېنوكسى ئاتسېتىك كىسلاتا</p>\n\n

三水铝石，三水铝矿	sān shuǐ lǚ dàn , sān shuǐ lǚ kuàng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">گىبسىت</p>\n\n
三法	sān fǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئۇسۇل، ئۈچ داۋالاش ئۇسۇلى</p>\n\n
三波脉	sān bō mài； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ دولقۇنلۇق تومۇر سوقۇش (پۇلس)</p>\n\n
三洋牌彩色电视机	三洋牌彩色电视机 （日）； sān yáng pái cǎi sè diàn shì jī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سانيو ماركىلىق رەڭلىك تېلېۋىزور</p>\n\n
三流戏院	sān liú xì yuàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">كىچىك تىياتىرخانا؛ سەييارە تىياتىر ئۆمىكى</p>\n\n
三流，三流的	sān liú , sān liú de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچىنچى ئېقىمدىكى، ئۈچىنچى ئېقىملىق؛ دەرىجىسى تۆۋەن</p>\n\n
三测向应变仪组	sān cè xiàng yìng biàn yí zǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">روزېتكا</p>\n\n
三浸式洗礼	sān jìn shì xǐ lǐ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قېتىملىق چوقۇنۇش</p>\n\n
三消	sān xiāo； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ يوقىتىش (كېسەللىك ئالامىتى)</p>\n\n
三溴乙醇	sān xiù yǐchún； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىبروموئېتانول</p>\n\n
三溴化合物	sān xiù huàhé wù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىبرومىد</p>\n\n
三溴化磷	sān xiù huà lín； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">فوسفور ترىبرومىد</p>\n\n
三灾八难	sān zāi bā nán； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئاپەت سەككىز مۈشكۈلات ( خۇراپاتلىق )؛  تۈرلۈك بالايىئاپەت؛ ئۈچ ئاپەت، سەككىز مۈشكۈلات</p>\n\n
三点交会分析径向三角测量	sān diǎn jiāo huì fēn xī jìng xiàng sān jiǎo cè liáng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ نۇقتىلىق ترىسېكسىيە ئانالىزى ئارقىلىق رادىئال ئۈچ بۇلۇڭ ئۆلچەش</p>\n\n
三点弯曲	sān diǎn wān qū； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ نۇقتىلىق ئېگىلىش</p>\n\n
三点曲线图	sān diǎn qǔ xiàn tú； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ نۇقتىلىق ئەگرى سىزىق سخېمىسى</p>\n\n
三点水，三点水儿	sāndiǎn shuǐ , sāndiǎn shuǐ ér； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">خەنزۇچە(خىتايچە) خەتنىڭ بۆلىكى</p>\n\n
三点法	sān diǎn fǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ نۇقتىلىق ئۇسۇل</p>\n\n
三点盲蝽	sāndiǎn máng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ داغلىق قارىغۇ چىرپاشكا</p>\n\n
三点着陆	sān diǎn zhe lù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ نۇقتىلىق قونۇش</p>\n\n
三点装	sān diǎn zhuāng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">بىكىنى سۇ ئۈزۈش كىيىمى</p>\n\n
三点西文活字	sān diǎn xī wén huó zì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">مىننىكىن (ئىسپانچە ئەڭ كىچىك نابور ھەرپى)</p>\n\n
三点透视	sān diǎn tòu shì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ نۇقتىلىق پېرسپېكتىۋ</p>\n\n
三点问题	sān diǎn wèn tí； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ نۇقتىلىق مەسىلە</p>\n\n
三烯	sān xī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىئېن؛ ترىئولېفىن</p>\n\n
三烷基的	三烷基［的］； sān wán jī de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىئالكىل</p>\n\n
三焦	sān jiāo； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سەنجياۋ (تىلنىڭ ئاستىدىن كۆكرەككىچە بولغان ئارىلىق)</p>\n\n
三焦俞	sān jiāo yú； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سەنجياۋشۇ (پەللە)</p>\n\n
三焦咳	sān jiāo ké； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سەنجياۋ يۆتىلى</p>\n\n
三焦病	sān jiāo bìng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سەنجياۋ كېسەللىرى</p>\n\n
三焦经	sān jiāo jīng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سەنجياۋ يوللىرى</p>\n\n
三焦胀	sān jiāo zhàng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">مەيدە كۆپۈش</p>\n\n
三焦距	sān jiāo jù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فوكۇسلۇق</p>\n\n
三焦辨证	sān jiāo biàn zhèng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سەنجياۋ پاتولوگىك ئۆزگىرىشى</p>\n\n
三熟	sān shú； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">3 قېتىم ھوسۇل ئېلىش؛ ئۈچ قېتىم پىششىق؛ ئۈچ قېتىم ھوسۇل ئېلىش</p>\n\n
三爪卡盘	sān zhǎo kǎ pán； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ پەنجىلىك دىسكا</p>\n\n
三爪虎耳草	sān zhǎo hǔ ěr cǎo； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بارماقلىق تاشيارغان</p>\n\n
三爪蚴	sān zhuǎ yòu； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ باسقۇچلۇق لىچىنكا</p>\n\n
三爷草	sān yé cǎo； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچقۇلاق</p>\n\n
三环烯，三环萜	sān huán xī , sān huán； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىسىكلېن</p>\n\n
三环的	sān huán de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىسىكلىك، ئۈچ ھالقىلىق</p>\n\n
三班制	sān bān zhì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئىسمېنىلىق تۈزۈم، ئۈچ ئىسمېنا تۈزۈمى؛ ئۈچ سمېنىلىق تۈزۈم</p>\n\n
三班循环作业采煤法	sān bān xún huán zuò yè cǎi méi fǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">3 سمېنا ئالمىشىپ كۆمۈر قېزىش ئۇسۇلى</p>\n\n
三球仪	sān qiú yí； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">قۇياش-يەر شارى-ئاي مودېلى</p>\n\n
三球悬铃木	sān qiú xuán líng mù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">چىنار</p>\n\n
三球悬铃木法国梧桐	三球悬铃木／法国梧桐（悬铃木科）； sān qiú xuán líng mù fǎ guó wú tóng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">شەرىق چىنار دەرىخى</p>\n\n
三球珍珠茅	sān qiú zhēn zhū máo； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىگلومېراتا ئېمپراتا قومۇشى</p>\n\n
三球韭	sān qiú jiǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىكوككۇم ياۋا كۈدىسى</p>\n\n
三瓣子嘴儿	三瓣［子］嘴儿； \nsān bàn zǐ zuǐ ér； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">توشقانكالپۇك بالا</p>\n\n

三瓣玖瑰线	sān bàn jiǔ guī xiàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بەرگلىك گۈل</p>\n\n
三瓦特计方法	sān wǎ tè jì fāng fǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ۋاتمېتر ئۇسۇلى</p>\n\n
三甘醇	sān gān chún； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىئېتىلېن گلىكول</p>\n\n
三生	sān shēng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ تۆرىلىش (بۇددا دىنىدا)</p>\n\n
三生层	sān shēng céng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلەمچى قەۋەت</p>\n\n
三生有幸	sān shēng yǒu xìng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">كۈتۈلمىگەن ئامەت، تەلىيى ئوڭدىن كېلىپ قالماق؛ قالتىس ئامەت؛  كارامەت بەخىت؛  تەلىيى ئوڭدىن كەلمەك</p>\n\n
三生细胞壁	sān shēng xì bāo bì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلەمچى ھۈجەيرە دىۋارى</p>\n\n
三用沙发	sān yòng shā fā； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ خىل ئىشلەتكىلى بولىدىغان سافا</p>\n\n
三田瓷器	sān tián cí qì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ساندا ساپال قاچىلىرى</p>\n\n

三界羊茅	三界羊茅（禾本科）； sān jiè yáng máo； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">يايلاق تىپچىقى</p>\n\n
三番两次	sān fān liǎng cì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">قايتا-قايتا، تەكرار-تەكرار، يېنىشلاپ-يېنىشلاپ</p>\n\n
三番五次	sān fān wǔ cì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">قايتا-قايتا؛ تەكرار-تەكرار؛ يېنىشلاپ-يېنىشلاپ؛ قايتا-قايتا، تەكرار-تەكرار؛ قايتا-قايتا؛  تەكرار-تەكرار؛  كەينى-كەينىدىن؛  نۇرغۇن قېتىم</p>\n\n
三番四复	sān fān sì fù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">قايتا-قايتا، تەكرار-تەكرار، يېنىشلاپ-يېنىشلاپ</p>\n\n
三痹	sān bì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ تىپلىق ئارترالگىيە</p>\n\n
三白草	sān bái cǎo； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سائۇرۇرۇس ئوتى</p>\n\n
三白草科	sān bái cǎo kē； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سائۇرۇرۇس ئوتى ئائىلىسى</p>\n\n
三百六十行	sān bǎi liù shí xíng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ھەممە ساھە-ھەممە كەسىپلەر</p>\n\n
三百六十行行行出状元	三百六十行，行行出状元； \nsān bǎi liù shí xíng xíng xíng chū zhuàng yuán； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ھەر ھۈنەرنىڭ باردۇر ئاقىدىغان يېرى، ھەر ھۈنەرنىڭ ئۆزىگە خاس ئۇستىسى-پىرى</p>\n\n
三皇	sān huáng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ پادىشاھ (رىۋايەتتىكى تيەنخۇاڭ، دىخۇاڭ، رېنخۇاڭلارنى كۆرسىتىدۇ)</p>\n\n
三相	sān xiāng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازىلىق؛ ئۈچ فازا، ئۈچ فازىلىق</p>\n\n
三相七线制	sān xiāng qī xiàn zhì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازا يەتتە سىملىق سىستېما</p>\n\n
三相三线制	sān xiāng sān xiàn zhì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازا ئۈچ سىملىق سىستېما؛ ئۈچ فازا-ئۈچ سىملىق سىستېما</p>\n\n
三相交变电流	三相[交变]电流； \nsān xiāng jiāo biàn diàn liú； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">3 فازىلىق ئۆزگىرىشچان توك</p>\n\n
三相交流电	sān xiāng jiāo liú diàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازىلىق ئۆزگىرىشچان توك؛ ئۈچ فازىلىق ئۆزگىرىشچان توك</p>\n\n
三相交流电动机	sān xiāng jiāo liú diàn dòng jī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازىلىق ئۆزگىرىشچان توك</p>\n\n
三相六线制	sān xiāng liù xiàn zhì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازا ئالتە سىملىق سىستېما</p>\n\n
三相半波	sān xiāng bàn bō； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازىلىق يېرىم دولقۇن</p>\n\n
三相发电机	sān xiāng fā diàn jī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازىلىق گېنېراتور؛ ئۈچ فازىلىق گېنېراتور</p>\n\n
三相变压器	sān xiāng biàn yā qì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازىلىق ترانسفورماتور</p>\n\n
三相四线制	sān xiāng sì xiàn zhì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازا-تۆت سىملىق سىستېما؛ ئۈچ فازا تۆت سىملىق سىستېما؛ ئۈچ فازىلىق تۆت سىملىق سىستېما</p>\n\n
三相四线制星形接法	sān xiāng sì xiàn zhì xīng xíng jiē fǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازىلىق تۆت سىملىق سىستېمىنى يۇلتۇز شەكلىدە ئۇلاش</p>\n\n
三相定子绕组	sān xiāng dìng zǐ rào zǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازىلىق ستاتورنىڭ ئورام گۇرۇپپىسى</p>\n\n
三相对称电流	sān xiāng duì chēng diàn liú； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازىلىق سىممېتىرىيىلىك-توك</p>\n\n
三相对称电源	sān xiāng duì chēng diàn yuán； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازىلىق سىممېتىرىيىلىك توك مەنبەسى</p>\n\n
三相对称电路	sān xiāng duì chēng diàn lù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازىلىق سىممېتىرىيىلىك توك يولى</p>\n\n
三相对称负载	sān xiāng duì chēng fù zǎi； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازىلىق سىممېتىرىيىلىك-يۈك</p>\n\n
三相异步电动机	sān xiāng yì bù diàn dòng jī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازىلىق ئاسىنخرون ماتور</p>\n\n
三相感应调节器	sān xiāng gǎn yīng tiáo jié qì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازىلىق ئىندۇكسىيە رېگۇلياتورى</p>\n\n
三相整流器	sān xiāng zhěng liú qì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازىلىق ئېقىم توغرىلىغۇچ</p>\n\n
三相旋转磁场	sān xiāng xuán zhuàn cí chǎng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازىلىق ئايلانما ماگىنىت مەيدانى</p>\n\n
三相比例	sān xiāng bǐ lì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ جىسىم نىسبىتى</p>\n\n
三相点	sān xiāng diǎn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازا نۇقتىسى</p>\n\n
三相熔断器	sān xiāng róng duàn qì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ فازىلىق ئېرىپ ئۈزۈلگۈچ</p>\n\n

三级实习指导教师	三级实习指导教师（初）； sān jí shí xí zhǐ dǎo jiào shī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">3-دەرىجىلىك پراكتىكا يېتەكچىسى</p>\n\n

三纲五常	sān gāng wǔ cháng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئەركان، بەش ئەھكام ( ئۈچ ئەركان: پۇقرانىڭ پادىشاھقا، خۇتۇننىڭ ئەرگە ۋە ئوغۇلنىڭ ئاتىغا يويسۇنۇشى. بەش ئەھكام: رەھىمدىللىك، ئىنساپ، ئەدەپ، پاراسەت ۋە سادىقلىق-ۋاپادارلىق )；ئۈچ ئەركان ۋە بەش ئەھكام</p>\n\n

三维表	sān wéi biǎo； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئۆلچەملىك جەدۋەل</p>\n\n
三维表示	sān wéi biǎo shì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئۆلچەملىك ئىپادىلەش</p>\n\n
三缄其口	sān jiān qí kǒu； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">زۇۋان سۈرمەسلىك؛ لام-جىم دېمەي قويماق؛ ئاغىزىنى پېچەتلەپ قويماق؛  سۆزدە ئېھتىياتچان بولماق</p>\n\n
三羟基乙胺硬脂酸酯	sān qiǎng jī yǐ àn yìng zhī suān zhǐ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىگىدروكسى ئېتىلامىن ستېئارات</p>\n\n
三羟基甲基蒽醌	sān qiǎng jī jiǎ jī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">گېلمىنتوسپورىن</p>\n\n
三羟铝石	sān qiǎng lǚ dàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">بايېرىت</p>\n\n
三羧酸	sān suōsuān； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىكاربوكسسىلىك كىسلاتا</p>\n\n
三羧酸脂	sān suōsuān zhī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىكاربوكسىلىك ئېستېر</p>\n\n
三翅的	sān chì de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قاناتلىق</p>\n\n
三翻四抖	sān fān sì dǒu； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئۆرۈپ، تۆت قېقىش (ئەلنەغمىدە ئىشلىتىدىغان سۆز)</p>\n\n
三翼机	sān yì jī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىپلان</p>\n\n
三老人	sān lǎo rén； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بوۋاي (چوسونلارنىڭ ئەلنەغمىسى)</p>\n\n
三联书写板	sān lián shū xiě bǎn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قاتلانما دوسكا</p>\n\n
三联剧	sān lián jù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قىسىملىق چاتما كومېدىيە</p>\n\n
三联单	sān lián dān； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك تالون؛ ئۈچ بەتلىك تالون</p>\n\n
三联投弹架	sān lián tóu dàn jià； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قاتلانما بومبا تاشلاش جازىسى</p>\n\n
三联炼钢法	sān lián liàn gāng fǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك پولات تاۋلاش ئۇسۇلى</p>\n\n
三联疫苗	sān lián yì miáo； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك ۋاكسىنا</p>\n\n
三聚乙硫醛	sān jù yǐ liú quán； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىتىئوئاتسېتالدېگىد</p>\n\n
三聚乙醛	sān jù yǐ quán； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">پارالدېگىد</p>\n\n
三聚作用	sān jù zuò yòng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىمېرلىشىش</p>\n\n
三聚异丁烯	sān jù yì dīng xī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترى ئىزوبۇتىلېن</p>\n\n
三聚氰胺树脂	sān jù qíng àn shù zhī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">مېلامىن سمولىسى</p>\n\n
三聚氰胺甲醛	sān jù qíng àn jiǎ quán； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">مېلامىن فورمالدېگىد</p>\n\n
三聚氰胺甲醛纸	sān jù qíng àn jiǎ quán zhǐ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">مېلامىن فورمالدېگىد قەغىزى</p>\n\n
三聚氰酸	sān jù qíng suān； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">پىرولىتىك كىسلاتا</p>\n\n
三聚物	sān jù wù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىمېر؛ ترىپولىمېر</p>\n\n
三聚的	sān jù de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىمېرىك، ترىمېرلىق</p>\n\n
三聚盐	sān jù yán； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىمېرلىق تۇز</p>\n\n
三聚磷酸钠	sān jù lín suān nà； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ناترىي ترىپولىفوسفات</p>\n\n
三肉豆蔻精	sān ròu dòu kòu jīng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىمىرىستىن</p>\n\n
三肋界	三肋界（菊科）； sān lèi jiè； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۇچۇرۇق</p>\n\n
三肠目	sān cháng mù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئۈچەيلىك قۇرتلار ئەترىتى</p>\n\n
三肢瘫痪	sān zhī tān huàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئىككى پۇت بىر قولى پالەچ بولۇش</p>\n\n
三肽	sān tài； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىپېپتىد</p>\n\n
三背的	sān bèi de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ يۆلەنچۈكلۈك</p>\n\n
三胚层动物	sān pēi céng dòng wù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىپلوبلاستلىق ھايۋانلار</p>\n\n
三胞胎	sān bāo tāi； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ گېزەك</p>\n\n
三胺	sān àn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىئامىن</p>\n\n
三能微波激射器	sān néng wēi bō jī shè qì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئىقتىدارلىق مازېر</p>\n\n
三能级激光器	sān néng jí jī guāng qì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئىقتىدارلىق لازېر</p>\n\n
三脉冲级联消除器	sān mài chōng jí lián xiāo chú qì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئىمپۇلسلىق تۇتىشىشنى يوقاتقۇچ</p>\n\n
三脉冲编码	sān mài chōng biān mǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئىمپۇلسلىق كودلاشتۇرۇش؛ ئۈچ ئىمپۇلسلىق كود</p>\n\n
三脚插头	sān jiǎo chā tóu； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ پۇتلۇق شتېپسېل؛ ئۈچ پۇتلۇق شتېپسىل</p>\n\n
三脚撑，三脚铁扒	sān jiǎo chēng , sān jiǎo tiě bā； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ پۇتلۇق تىرەك، ئۈچ پۇتلۇق ئىسكاپ</p>\n\n
三脚架	sān jiǎo jià； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ۋېشكا، موسى ياغاچ؛ ئۈچ پۇتلۇق جازا؛ ئۈچ پۇتلۇق جازا؛ ئۈچ پۇتلۇق جازا، ئۈچ پۇتلۇق تىرەك</p>\n\n
三脚架拔桩机	sān jiǎo jià bá zhuāng jī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ پۇتلۇق قوزۇق يۇلۇش ماشىنىسى</p>\n\n
三脚桌	sān jiǎo zhuō； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ پۇتلۇق ئۈستەل</p>\n\n
三脚的	sān jiǎo de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ پۇتلۇق</p>\n\n
三脚起重机	sān jiǎo qǐ zhòng jī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ پۇتلۇق كران</p>\n\n
三脚起重架	sān jiǎo qǐ zhòng jià； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ پۇتلۇق كران</p>\n\n
三脚钻机	sān jiǎo zuàn jī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ پۇتلۇق بۇرغىلاش ماشىنىسى</p>\n\n
三脲	sān； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىئۇرېت</p>\n\n
三臂分度规	sān bì fēn dù guī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ يەلكىلىك شكالىلارغا بۆلگۈچ پەركا</p>\n\n
三色	sān sè； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ رەڭلىك؛ ئۈچ خىل رەڭ</p>\n\n
三色介代花	三色介代花（花葱科）； sān sè jiè dài huā； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">چىرانگۈل</p>\n\n
三色刺激值	sān sè cì jī zhí； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قوزغاتقۇچ رەڭ قىممىتى</p>\n\n
三色刺激的	sān sè cì jī de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قوزغاتقۇچ رەڭلىك</p>\n\n
三色反常症	sān sè fǎn cháng zhèng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">نورمالسىز ترىخروماتىزم، ئۈچ خىل رەڭنى پەرق قىلالماسلىق نورمالسىزلىق كېسىلى</p>\n\n
三色叠加镜	sān sè dié jiā jìng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">فوتوخروموسكوپ</p>\n\n
三色吉莉草	sān sè jí lì cǎo； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ رەڭلىك گىلىيە ئوتى</p>\n\n
三色堇	sān sè jǐn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">كېپىنەكگۈل؛ ئىنسىگۈل، كېپنەكگۈل</p>\n\n
三色堇紫红色	sān sè jǐn zǐ hóngsè； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">قېنىق قىزغۇچ سۆسۈن رەڭ</p>\n\n
三色堇色	sān sè jǐn sè； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">قېنىق سۆسۈن رەڭ</p>\n\n
三色学说	sān sè xué shuō； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ رەڭ تەلىماتى</p>\n\n
三色性	sān sè xìng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىخروماتىزم، ئۈچ رەڭلىك</p>\n\n
三色摄影	sān sè shè yǐng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ رەڭ فوتوگرافىيىسى</p>\n\n
三色旗	sān sè qí； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ رەڭلىك بايراق</p>\n\n
三色松叶菊	三色松叶菊（番舌科）； sān sè sōng yè jú； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">گۈلقەيۇر</p>\n\n
三色法	sān sè fǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ رەڭلىك بېسىش ئۇسۇلى</p>\n\n
三色测光	sān sè cè guāng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ رەڭ فوتومېترىيىسى</p>\n\n
三色滤光屏	sān sè lǜ guāng píng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ خىل رەڭنى سۈزۈش ئېكرانى</p>\n\n
三色版	sān sè bǎn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ خىل رەڭلىك بەت</p>\n\n
三色理论	sān sè lǐ lùn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ رەڭ نەزەرىيىسى</p>\n\n
三色碳溴法	sān sè tàn xiù fǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ رەڭلىك كاربون بروم ئۇسۇلى</p>\n\n
三色色标管	sān sè sè biāo guǎn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ رەڭلىك خروماترون</p>\n\n
三色花的	sān sè huā de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ خىل رەڭلىك ئالا</p>\n\n
三色苋	sān sè xiàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئالابۇغداش؛ قىزىل بۇغداش</p>\n\n
三色菊	三色菊（菊科）； sān sè jú； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">رەناگۈل</p>\n\n
三色蛋	sān sè dàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئارىلاشما تۇخۇم دۈملىمىسى</p>\n\n
三色视觉者	sān sè shì jué zhě； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ رەڭنى ئېنىق تونۇغۇچى</p>\n\n
三节棍	sān jié gùn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بوغۇملۇق كالتەك</p>\n\n
三节点式的	sān jié diǎn shì de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بوغۇملۇق</p>\n\n
三节蜂科	sān jié fēng kē； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئارگىد ھەرىلىرى ئائىلىسى</p>\n\n
三芒草	sān máng cǎo； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">پەيقىلتىرىق؛ ئاق سېلېۋ، پەيقىلتىرىق</p>\n\n
三芒草属	sān máng cǎo shǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئاق سېلەۋ ئۇرۇقدىشى</p>\n\n
三芯同轴电缆	sān xīn tóng zhóu diàn lǎn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئۆزەكلىك ئورتاق ئوقلۇق كابېل</p>\n\n
三芯电缆	sān xīn diàn lǎn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئۆزەكلىك كابېل</p>\n\n
三花属	sān huā shǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ گۈللۈكلەر ئۇرۇقدىشى</p>\n\n
三花柱的	sān huā zhù de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ گۈل ساپىقىلىق</p>\n\n
三花桉	sān huā ān； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئاق ماخوگانىيە دەرىخى؛ ئاۋسترالىيە ئېۋكالىپت دەرىخى</p>\n\n
三花瓣状的	sān huā bàn zhuàng de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ گۈلتاج شەكىللىك</p>\n\n
三花瓣的	sān huā bàn de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ گۈلتاجلىق</p>\n\n
三花聚顶	sān huā jù dǐng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">زېھىنىنى يىغىش</p>\n\n
三花脸	sān huā liǎn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ھەييار، ھەزىلكەش، قىزىقچى (سېركتە)</p>\n\n
三花路边青，三花水场梅	sān huā lùbiān qīng , sān huā shuǐ chǎng méi； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ گۈللۈك سۇ بۆلجۈرگىنى</p>\n\n
三芳基甲烷染料	sān fāng jī jiǎ wán rǎn liào； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىئارىل مېتان بويىقى</p>\n\n
三芳基的	sān fāng jī de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىئارىل</p>\n\n
三苯基	三苯［基］； sān běn jī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىفېنىل</p>\n\n
三苯基四唑氯	sān běn jī sì zuò lǜ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىفېنىل تېترازول خلورىد</p>\n\n

三角形	三角形（△tri angle）； sān jiǎo xíng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچبۇلۇڭ؛ ئۈچ بۇلۇڭ؛ ئۈچ بۇلۇڭ، ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق</p>\n\n
三角形三	sān jiǎo xíng sān； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئارترىيە، جەنۇبتىكى ئەلفا ئۈچ بۇلۇڭى، ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق ئۈچ سىستېما، ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق ئۈچ يۇلتۇزلار سىستېمىسى</p>\n\n
三角形信号	sān jiǎo xíng xìn hào； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭ شەكىللىك سىگنال</p>\n\n
三角形偶极子	sān jiǎo xíng ǒu jí zǐ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق دىپول</p>\n\n

三角形匹配天线	sān jiǎo xíng pǐ pèi tiān xiàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">لايىقلاشتۇرغۇچى ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق ئانتېننا</p>\n\n
三角形天帆	sān jiǎo xíng tiān fān； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇرجەك يەلكەن</p>\n\n
三角形天线	sān jiǎo xíng tiān xiàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق ئانتېننا</p>\n\n
三角形截面踏步	sān jiǎo xíng jié miàn tà bù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">كەسمە يۈزى ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق باسقۇچ</p>\n\n
三角形接法	sān jiǎo xíng jiē fǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭ شەكلىدە ئۇلاش ئۇسۇلى؛ 3 بۇلۇڭ شەكلىدە ئۇلاش؛ ئۈچ بۇرجەك شەكلىدە چېتىش</p>\n\n
三角形数	sān jiǎo xíng shù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇرجەك تىزىلغان رەقەملەر</p>\n\n
三角形木料堆	sān jiǎo xíng mù liào duī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قىرلىق ياغاچ دۆۋىسى</p>\n\n
三角形构架	sān jiǎo xíng gòu jià； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق قۇرۇلما</p>\n\n
三角形枪显象管	sān jiǎo xíng qiāng xiǎn xiàng guǎn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">دېلتىسىمان تەسۋىر كۆرسەتكۈچ تۇرۇبا</p>\n\n
三角形楣饰	sānjiǎoxíng méi shì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق ماڭلاي ياغاچ بېزىكى</p>\n\n
三角形法	sān jiǎo xíng fǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭ ئۇسۇلى</p>\n\n
三角形电流	sān jiǎo xíng diàn liú； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق توك</p>\n\n
三角形电路	sān jiǎo xíng diàn lù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق توك يولى</p>\n\n
三角形的内切圆	sān jiǎo xíng de nèi qiē yuán； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭغا ئىچتىن تېگىشكەن چەمبەر</p>\n\n
三角形的外心	sān jiǎo xíng de wai xīn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭنىڭ سىرتقى مەركىزى</p>\n\n
三角形的旁切圆	sān jiǎo xíng de páng qiē yuán； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭغا ياندىن تېگىشكەن چەمبەر</p>\n\n
三角形网络	sān jiǎo xíng wǎng luò； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇرجەك تور؛ ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق تور</p>\n\n
三角形脉冲	sān jiǎo xíng mài chōng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭ شەكىللىك ئىمپۇلس؛ ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق ئىمپۇلس</p>\n\n
三角形脉冲函数	sān jiǎo xíng mài chōng hán shù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق ئىمپۇلس فۇنكسىيىسى</p>\n\n
三角形连接法	sān jiǎo xíng lián jiē fǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچبۇلۇڭ شەكلىدە ئۇلاش ئۇسۇلى</p>\n\n

三角恋爱	sān jiǎo liàn ài； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇرجەك مۇھەببەتلىشىش</p>\n\n

三角支架	sān jiǎo zhī jià； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇرجەك شتاتىۋ؛ ئۈچ بۇرجەك تىرەك</p>\n\n
三角方程	sān jiǎo fāng chéng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىگونومېتىرىيىلىك تەڭلىمە؛ ترىگونومېترىيىلىك تەڭلىمە</p>\n\n

三角果属	sān jiǎo guǒ shǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قىرلىق مېۋىلىكلەر ئۇرۇقدىشى</p>\n\n

三角枫	三角枫（槭树科）； sān jiǎo fēng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">بېگىر ئىرەن دەرىخى؛ غاز تاپان ئېرەك؛ ئۈچ بۇرجەك ئېرەن دەرىخى</p>\n\n
三角架	sān jiǎo jià； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ۋېشكا، ئۈچ پۇتلۇق جازا، ئۈچ پۇتلۇق تىرەك، موسى ياغاچ</p>\n\n
三角架立杆法	sān jiǎo jià lì gǎn fǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق جازا ئارقىلىق ستولبا تىكلەش ئۇسۇلى</p>\n\n
三角柱兽亚目	sān jiǎo zhù shòu yà mù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىگونوستىلوپودىيە ئەترىتى</p>\n\n

三角测高器	sān jiǎo cè gāo qì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">گىپسومېتر</p>\n\n

三角背心	sān jiǎo bèi xīn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">خالتېر (ئۈچ بۇلۇڭسىمان مايكا)</p>\n\n
三角脉冲	sān jiǎo mài chōng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق شەكىللىك ئىمپۇلس</p>\n\n

三角螺纹	sān jiǎo luó wén； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">V شەكىللىك رېزبا</p>\n\n

三角裤	sān jiǎo kù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترۇسىك (پۇچقاقسىز كالتە ئىشتان)</p>\n\n
三角规，三脚规	sānjiǎo guī , sān jiǎo guī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق كومپاس، ئۈچ پۇتلۇق كومپاس</p>\n\n
三角视差	sān jiǎo shì chà； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىگونومېترىيىلىك پاراللاكس</p>\n\n
三角解	sān jiǎo jiě； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىگونومېترىيىلىك يېشىش</p>\n\n
三角记号	sān jiǎo jì hào； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق بەلگە</p>\n\n
三角贸易	sān jiǎo mào yì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇرجەك سودا؛ 3 تەرەپلىك سودا</p>\n\n
三角辅助帆	sān jiǎo fǔ zhù fān； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇرجەك قوشۇمچە يەلكەن</p>\n\n
三角选举区	sān jiǎo xuǎn jǔ qū； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇرجەك سايلام رايونى</p>\n\n
三角钉	sān jiǎo dìng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">تىكەنلىك سىم</p>\n\n
三角铁	sān jiǎo tiě； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قىرلىق تۆمۈر</p>\n\n
三角锉	sānjiǎo cuò； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">3 قىرلىق ئېكەك؛ ئۈچ قىرلىق ئېكەك</p>\n\n
三角锯锉	sānjiǎo jū cuò； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قىرلىق ھەرە ئېكىكى</p>\n\n
三角阔裂豆	sān jiǎo kuò liè dòu； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇرجەك كەڭ يېرىلغان پۇرچاق</p>\n\n
三角面	sān jiǎo miàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇرجەك يۈز</p>\n\n
三角韧带	sān jiǎo rèn dài； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇرجەك سىڭىر</p>\n\n
三角顶帆	sān jiǎo dǐng fān； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇلۇڭ چوققىلىق يەلكەن</p>\n\n
三角饰	sān jiǎo shì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇرجەك بېزەك</p>\n\n
三角饺子	sān jiǎo jiǎo zǐ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بۇرجەك جۇۋاۋا</p>\n\n
三角验袋法	sān jiǎo yàn dài fǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">تاغارنى ئۇچ بۇلۇڭ شەكلىگە كەلتۈرۈپ تەكشۈرۈش ئۇسۇلى</p>\n\n
三角骨	sān jiǎo gǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">پىرامىدىسىمان سۆڭەك (بېغىش سۆڭىكىنىڭ بىرى)</p>\n\n
三角高程测量法	sān jiǎo gāo chéng cè liáng fǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىگونومېترىيىلىك ئېگىزلىك ئۆلچەش ئۇسۇلى</p>\n\n
三角龙属	sān jiǎo lóng shǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ مۈڭگۈزلۈك دىنوزاۋر ئۇرۇقدىشى</p>\n\n
三解韵格	sān jiě yùn gé； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">باللادا</p>\n\n
三言两语	sān yán liǎng yǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">بىرەر-ئىككى ئېغىز گەپ؛  بىر نەچچە ئېغىز سۆز</p>\n\n
三言两语，三言两句	sān yán liǎng yǔ , sān yán liǎng jù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">قىسقىغىنا؛ مۇختەسەر قىلىپ؛ بىر-ئىككى ئېغىز سۆز بىلەن</p>\n\n
三言语	sān yán yǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">قىسقىغىنا؛ بىر-ئىككى ئېغىز سۆز بىلەن؛ مۇختەسەر قىلىپ</p>\n\n
三讲教育回头看	sān jiǎng jiào yù huí tóu kàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">3 كە ئەھمىيەت بېرىش تەربىيىسىدىن كېيىنكى تەكشۈرۈش</p>\n\n
三讲讲学习讲政治讲正气教育	三讲（讲学习，讲政治，讲正气）教育； \nsān jiǎng jiǎng xué xí jiǎng zhèng zhì jiǎng zhèng qì jiào yù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">3 كە ئەھمىيەت بېرىش (ئۆگىنىشكە، سىياسىيغا، توغرا كەيپىياتقا ئەھمىيەت بېرىش) تەربىيىسى</p>\n\n
三论宗	sān lùn zōng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سانرون (دىنىي مەزھەپ)</p>\n\n
三语种的	sān yǔ zhǒng de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ تىللىق</p>\n\n
三资企业	sān zī qǐ yè； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ خىل مەبلەغ بىلەن قۇرۇلغان كارخانا؛ ئۈچ خىل شەكىلدىكى كارخانىلار؛ 3 خىل شەكىلدىكى كارخانىلار</p>\n\n
三足行走	sān zú xíng zǒu； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ پۇتلۇق مېڭىش</p>\n\n
三足赛跑	sān zú sài pǎo； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ پۇتلۇق يۈگۈرۈش مۇسابىقىسى</p>\n\n
三足鼎立	sān zú dǐng lì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ پۇتلۇق داڭقان؛ داڭقان پۇتىدەك روبىرو تۇرماق؛  ئۈچ تەرەپ تىركىشىپ تۇرماق</p>\n\n
三趾啄木鸟	sān zhǐ zhuó mù niǎo； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ پەنجىلىك تۆمۈر تۇمشۇق؛ ئۈچ بارماقلىق تۆمۈر تۇمشۇق</p>\n\n
三趾形超科	sān zhǐ xíng chāo kē； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ پەنجىلىكلەر سۇپېر ئائىلىسى</p>\n\n
三趾树懒	sān zhǐ shù lǎn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بارماقلىق لېنىۋېتىس</p>\n\n
三趾的	sān zhǐ de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ بارماقلىق، ئۈچ پەنجىلىك</p>\n\n
三趾马属	sān zhǐ mǎ shǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">قەدىمكى گىپپارىيون؛ ئۈچ تۇياقلىق ئات</p>\n\n
三趾鸥	sān zhǐ ōu； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ پەنجىلىك چايكا</p>\n\n
三趾鹑	sān zhǐ chún； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سۇ بۆدۈنىسى</p>\n\n
三趾鹑属	sān zhǐ chún shǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سۇ بۆدۈنىسى ئۇرۇقدىشى</p>\n\n
三趾鹬	sān zhǐ yù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">بارماقلىق قىليورغا؛ ئۈچ پەنجىلىك لايخورەك</p>\n\n
三跋罗	sān bá luó； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">پروخىبىت (سانسكرىتچە پەرھىز)</p>\n\n
三跑田	sān pǎo tián； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ توختىمايدىغان ئېتىز</p>\n\n
三距矮翠雀	sān jù ǎi cuì què； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ گۈلتاجلىق دېلفىنىئۇم ئوتى</p>\n\n
三路布局	sān lù bù jú； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ يوللۇق ئورۇنلاشتۇرۇش</p>\n\n
三路开关	sān lù kāi guān； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ يوللۇق ۋىكليۇچاتېل</p>\n\n
三路接线盒	sān lù jiē xiàn hé； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ يوللۇق سىم ئۇلاش كوروپكىسى</p>\n\n
三路载波	sān lù zǎi bō； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ يوللۇق يۈكلىمە دولقۇن</p>\n\n
三路通信制	sān lù tōng xìn zhì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ يوللۇق خەۋەرلىشىش سىستېمىسى</p>\n\n
三身	sān shēn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىكايا (بۇددا دىنىدا)</p>\n\n
三身翼水母属	sān shēn yì shuǐ mǔ shǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">گېريونىيە ئوتى</p>\n\n
三轨制	sān guǐ zhì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ يول سىستېمىسى، ئۈچ رېلس سىستېمىسى</p>\n\n
三轮	sān lún； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ چاقلىق</p>\n\n
三轮人力车	sān lún rén lì chē； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ چاقلىق قول ھارۋا</p>\n\n
三轮摩托车	sān lún mó tuō chē； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ چاقلىق موتسىكلىت</p>\n\n
三轮滑车组	sān lún huá chē zǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ چاقلىق غالتەكلەر گۇرۇپپىسى</p>\n\n
三轮童车	sān lún tóng chē； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ چاقلىق بالىلار ۋېلىسىپىتى</p>\n\n
三轮车	sān lún chē； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ چاقلىق ۋېلىسىپىت، ئۈچ چاقلىق ماشىنا، ئۈچ چاقلىق رىكشا؛ 3 چاقلىق ۋېلىسىپىت (ماشىنا، موتسىكىلىت)；ئۈچ چاقلىق رىكشا</p>\n\n
三轮送货车	sān lún sòng huò chē； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ چاقلىق ۋېلىسىپىت</p>\n\n
三轮齿轴	sān lún chǐ zhóu； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ چاقلىق چىىشلىق ئوق</p>\n\n
三轴卫星	sān zhóu wèi xīng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئوقلۇق سۈنئىي ھەمراھ</p>\n\n
三轴模拟器	sān zhóu mó nǐ qì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئوقلۇق تەقلىدلەشتۈرگۈچ</p>\n\n
三轴骨针	sān zhóu gǔ zhēn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىئاكسون (بۇلۇتنىڭ ئۈچ ئوقلۇق سۆڭىكى)</p>\n\n
三辊轧机	sān gǔn zhá jī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ تۇلۇقلۇق يانجىش ماشىنىسى</p>\n\n
三边	sān biān； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ تەرەپ</p>\n\n
三边形	sān biān xíng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ تەرەپلىك، ئۈچ بۇلۇڭلۇق؛ ئۈچ تەرەپلىك</p>\n\n
三边形凸肚窗	sān biān xíng tū dù chuāng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ تەرەپلىك كۆپمە دېرىزە</p>\n\n
三边测量	sān biān cè liáng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ تەرەپلىك ئۆلچەش</p>\n\n
三边贸易	sān biān mào yì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">3 تەرەپلىك سودا؛ ئۈچ تەرەپلىك سودا</p>\n\n
三过磷酸钙	sān guò lín suān gài； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">كالتسىي ترى سۇپېرفوسفات</p>\n\n
三进制	sān jìn zhì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك سىستېما؛ ئۈچلۈك ساناق سىستېمىسى</p>\n\n
三进制代码	sān jìn zhì dài mǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك سىستېما كودى</p>\n\n
三进制增量表示法	sān jìn zhì zēng liàng biǎo shì fǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك ساناق سىستېمىسىدىكى ئاشما مىقدارنى ئىپادىلەش</p>\n\n
三进制码	sān jìn zhì mǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك ساناق سىستېمىسىدىكى كود</p>\n\n
三进制脉码调制	sān jìn zhì mài mǎ diào zhì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك ساناق سىستېمىسىدىكى ئىمپۇلس كودىنىڭ تەڭشىلىشى</p>\n\n
三进制计数器	sān jìn zhì jì shù qì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك سىستېمىدىكى سانىغۇچ</p>\n\n
三进制记数法	sān jìn zhì jì shù fǎ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك سىستېمىدا خاتىرىلەش ئۇسۇلى</p>\n\n
三进制运算	sān jìn zhì yùn suàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك سىستېمىدا ھېسابلاش</p>\n\n
三进展开	sān jìn zhǎn kāi； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك يېيىش</p>\n\n
三连冠	sān lián guàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۇدا ئۈچ قېتىم چېمپىئون بولماق</p>\n\n
三连晶	sān lián jīng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ تۇتاش كرىستاللىق</p>\n\n
三连的	sān lián de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك</p>\n\n
三连襟	三连襟（儿）； sān lián jīn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچىنچى باجا</p>\n\n
三连音	sān lián yīn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">تۇتاش ئۈچ ئاھاڭ</p>\n\n
三连音符	sān lián yīn fú； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئاھاڭنى تۇتاشتۇرۇش بەلگىسى</p>\n\n
三通	sān tōng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ئالاقە؛ ئۈچ باشلىق چاتقۇ؛ 3 باشلىق چاتقۇ، 3 ئالاقە</p>\n\n
三通天线转发开关	sān tōng tiān xiàn zhuǎn fā kāi guān； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ باشلىق ئانتېننا ئايلاندۇرۇش ۋىكليۇچاتېلى</p>\n\n
三通开关	sān tōng kāi guān； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ يوللۇق ۋېكليۇچاتېل</p>\n\n
三通管	sān tōng guǎn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ باشلىق چاتقۇ</p>\n\n
三通道	sān tōng dào； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قانال</p>\n\n
三通阀	sān tōng fá； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ باشلىق جۈمەك</p>\n\n
三道体区	sān dào tǐ qū； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ تىكەن پالاقچە (تىكەن تېرىلىكلەرنىڭ)</p>\n\n
三道坝乡	三道坝乡【新疆各地】； sān dào bà xiāng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سەنداۋبا يېزىسى</p>\n\n
三道桥乡	三道桥乡【新疆各地】； sān dào qiáo xiāng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچئۆستەڭ يېزىسى</p>\n\n
三道河子乡	三道河子乡【新疆各地】； sān dào hé zǐ xiāng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سەندۇخوزا يېزىسى</p>\n\n
三道河子镇	三道河子镇【新疆各地】； sān dào hé zǐ zhèn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سەندوخوزا بازىرى</p>\n\n
三道防线	sān dào fáng xiàn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ لىنىيىلىك مۇداپىئە</p>\n\n
三部九候	sān bù jiǔ hòu； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">قەدىمكى پۇتۇن بەدەننى تەكشۈرۈپ دىئاگنوز قويۇش ئۇسۇلى</p>\n\n
三部曲	sān bù qǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىلوگىيە</p>\n\n
三部虫门	sān bù chóng mén； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">پرىئاپۇلىد قۇرتى تىپى</p>\n\n
三酚	sān fēn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىفېنول</p>\n\n

三醇	sān chún； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىئول</p>\n\n
三醋酯纤维	sān cù zhǐ xiān wéi； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىئاتسېتات، سېلليۇلوزا ترىئاتسېتات تالاسى</p>\n\n
三醋酸纤维素	sān cù suān xiān wéi sù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">سېلليۇلوزا ترىئاتسېتات</p>\n\n
三醋酸酯	sān cù suān zhǐ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىئاتسېتات</p>\n\n
三重	sān zhòng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ كىشىلىك، ئۈچ قات، ئۈچ تەكرار؛ ئۈچ قاتلانغان</p>\n\n
三重协奏曲	sān zhòng xié zòu qǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ خىل چالغۇ تەڭكەش قىلىنىپ چېلىنىدىغان كۈي</p>\n\n
三重反应	sān zhòng fǎn yīng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك رېئاكسىيە</p>\n\n
三重唱，三重唱曲	sānchóng chàng , sānchóng chàng qū； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ كىشىلىك ناخشا</p>\n\n
三重奏鸣曲	sān zhòng zòu míng qǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ خىل چالغۇ تەڭكەش قىلىنىپ چېلىنىدىغان كۈي</p>\n\n
三重奏，三重奏曲	sānchóng zòu , sānchóng zòu qū； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك كۈي</p>\n\n
三重婚	sān zhòng hūn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ خوتۇنلۇق ياكى ئۈچ ئەرلىك نىكاھ؛ ترىگامىيە، ئۈچ قېتىم توي قىلىش</p>\n\n
三重对位	sān zhòng duì wèi； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك ماس نۇقتا</p>\n\n
三重态	sān zhòng tai； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">3 قات ھالەت؛ ئۈچلۈك ھالەت</p>\n\n
三重数量积	三重数［量］积； \nsān zhòng shù liàng jī； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك سان يىغىندىسى</p>\n\n
三重星系	sān zhòng xīng xì； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قاتلاملىق يۇلتۇزلار سىستېمىسى</p>\n\n
三重杀	sān zhòng shā； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك ئويناش</p>\n\n

三重比圆	sān zhòng bǐ yuán； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قات نىسبەت چەمبىرى</p>\n\n
三重点	sān zhòng diǎn； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قاتلانغان نۇقتا</p>\n\n
三重碰撞	sān zhòng pèng zhuàng； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ زەرەتنىڭ بىرلا ۋاقىتتا ئۆزئارا سوقۇلۇشى</p>\n\n
三重结构记录	sān zhòng jié gòu jì lù； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قات قۇرۇلمىلىق خاتىرىلەش</p>\n\n
三重胚的	sān zhòng pēi de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ترىپلوبلاستىك</p>\n\n
三重表达	sān zhòng biǎo dá； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قات ئىپادىلەش</p>\n\n
三重赋格曲	sān zhòng fù gé qǔ； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچلۈك فۇگۋې كۈيى</p>\n\n

三重链滑车	sān zhòng liàn huá chē； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قاتلانما زەنجىرلىك غالتەك</p>\n\n
三重频带	sān zhòng pín dài； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ قات چاستوتا بەلۋېغى</p>\n\n
三钙的	sān gài de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ كالتسىي ئاتومىلىق</p>\n\n
三钠的	三钠［的］； sān nà de； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">ئۈچ ناترىيلىق</p>\n\n
三锥象虫科	sān zhuī xiàng chóng kē； \n<p style="direction:rtl; text-indent=30px; color: #FF8000; font-family:AdobeNaskh-Medium; font-size:18px;">برېنتۇس چېرېپاشكىسى ئائىلىسى</p>\n\n
